Each method has a product-level and trade-level pricer:\\n\\n1. **BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java) - Prices `ResolvedFxVanillaOption` using Black's formula with lognormal volatilities. Uses `DiscountingFxSingleProductPricer` for underlying FX pricing.\\n\\n2. **BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java) - Prices `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade` by combining product pricing and payment discounting using `DiscountingPaymentPricer`.\\n\\n3. **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java) - Prices `ResolvedFxVanillaOption` using the Vanna-Volga method, which adjusts Black prices for implied volatility smile effects.\\n\\n4. **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java) - Prices `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade` using Vanna-Volga method with payment discounting.\\n\\n### Measure Calculation Layer (modules/measure)\\nThe calculation engine layer wires pricers to measure computation:\\n\\n1. **FxVanillaOptionMethod** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionMethod.java) - An enum with values BLACK and VANNA_VOLGA that controls which pricer to use for calculations.
